    (function () {
        function initializeHeader() {
            if (window.IS24 && IS24.core && IS24.core.extensions && IS24.core.extensions.topnavigation) {
                IS24.core.extensions.topnavigation.init();
            }
        }

        if (
            document.readyState === "complete" ||
            (document.readyState !== "loading" && !document.documentElement.doScroll)
        ) {
            // execute immediately if DOMContentLoaded has already fired
            // this is a fallback for applications which load the header asynchronously and need to execute this script after DOM Ready
            initializeHeader();
        } else {
            if ("addEventListener" in document) {
                document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
                    initializeHeader();
                });
            } else if ("attachEvent" in document) {
                document.attachEvent("onreadystatechange", function () {
                    if (document.readyState === "complete") {
                        initializeHeader();
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    }());
      </script>

       (function () {
                function initializeLoginBox() {

                (document.readyState !== "loading" && !document.documentElement.doScroll)
                ) {
                        // execute immediately if DOMContentLoaded has already fired
                        // this is a fallback for applications which load the header asynchronously and need to execute this script after DOM Ready
                        initializeLoginBox();
                    } else {
                        if ("addEventListener" in document) {
                        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
                        initializeLoginBox();
                        });
                    } else if ("attachEvent" in document) {

      <script type="text/javascript">
       function loadNotificationWidgetScript() {
          IS24.STATIC.helpers.loadScript("//notification-center.recommendation.immobilienscout24.de/widget/stable/js/is24-header-notification-widget.js", {async: true});
      }

      function loadNotificationWidget() {
          loadNotificationWidgetScript();
          sessionStorage.setItem('userInteraction', 1);
          ["mousemove", "touchstart"].forEach(function (event) {
              window.removeEventListener(event, loadNotificationWidget);
          });
      }

      if (!sessionStorage.getItem('userInteraction')) {
          ["mousemove", "touchstart"].forEach(function (event) {
              window.addEventListener(event, loadNotificationWidget);
          });
      } else {
          loadNotificationWidgetScript();
      }
